if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') != 'f3c6f8cef7421152f3d4634bb7c65a822c171a42') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== 'f3c6f8cef7421152f3d4634bb7c65a822c171a42') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== 'b881deeb534152eea5712b063e8e759f87947a54') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== 'f3c6f8cef7421152f3d4634bb7c65a822c171a42') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php') != '7f63ed8db29535e1912aaa26b1948a05f98e206b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php') !== '7f63ed8db29535e1912aaa26b1948a05f98e206b') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php') !== 'd1537c03fd396ff213dfb43ca784b4d04f5cbca4') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php') !== '7f63ed8db29535e1912aaa26b1948a05f98e206b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/objectTypes/doi/OIDplusDoi.class.php');
		}
	}
}

	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/other/OIDplusOther.class.php') != 'b5aed30da3f11e481d85324c40bdf27eeb8678bb') {

	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/objectTypes/other/OIDplusOther.class.php', 0644)) {

	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/objectTypes/other/OIDplusOther.class.php') !== 'b5aed30da3f11e481d85324c40bdf27eeb8678bb') {
